    // Block all Ezoic/Aldesrv calls that are breaking the site
    (function() {
        var blockDomains = ['aldesrv.com', 'ezoic.net', 'ezoimgfmt.com'];
        var originalFetch = window.fetch;
        var originalXHR = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open;
        
        // Block fetch
        window.fetch = function(url) {
            if (blockDomains.some(domain => url.includes(domain))) {
                console.log('Blocked Ezoic ghost call:', url);
                return Promise.reject('Blocked Ezoic');
            }
            return originalFetch.apply(this, arguments);
        };
        
        // Block XHR
        XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open = function(method, url) {
            if (blockDomains.some(domain => url.includes(domain))) {
                console.log('Blocked Ezoic XHR:', url);
                return;
            }
            return originalXHR.apply(this, arguments);
        };
    })();
    </script>

    (function() {
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const tables = document.querySelectorAll('.wpDataTable');
        if (!tables.length) return;

        const tableCount = tables.length;
        console.log('GCBC: Found ' + tableCount + ' tables - applying SAFE throttling');

        // --- SAFE wrapper: do NOT swallow handlers; just pass through ---
        const originalAdd = EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener;
        if (!originalAdd.__gcbcWrapped) {
          EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener = function(type, listener, options) {
            // Let all listeners attach normally (resize/scroll included)
            return originalAdd.call(this, type, listener, options);
          };
          EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener.__gcbcWrapped = true;
        }

        // Remove ONLY specific, known-problem namespaces (never blanket .off())
        if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
          const $w = jQuery(window), $d = jQuery(document);
          const badNS = [
            'scroll.wpDataTables','resize.wpDataTables',
            'scroll.datatables','resize.datatables',
            'scroll.fixedHeader','resize.fixedHeader',
            'scroll.responsive','resize.responsive',
            'scroll.dtfh','resize.dtfh'
          ];
          badNS.forEach(ns => { $w.off(ns); $d.off(ns); });
        }

        // Minimal scroll handler (only when many tables). Attach using the original addEventListener.
        if (tableCount >= 3) {
          let raf = null, last = 0;
          function minimalScrollHandler() {
            if (raf) return;
            raf = requestAnimationFrame(function() {
              const now = Date.now();
              if (now - last >= 100) {
                // intentionally minimal work
              }
              last = now;
              raf = null;
            });
          }
          originalAdd.call(window, 'scroll', minimalScrollHandler, { passive: true });
        }

        // Disable heavy DataTables features without impacting chart init
        if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined' && jQuery.fn.dataTable) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            jQuery('.wpDataTable').each(function() {
              try {
                const table = jQuery(this).DataTable();
                if (table.fixedHeader) table.fixedHeader.disable();
                if (table.responsive) table.responsive.recalc = function() { return false; };
                if (table.columns && table.columns.adjust) {
                  table.columns.adjust = function() { return false; };
                }
              } catch(e) {
                console.log('DT feature disable error:', e);
              }
            });

            // Final cleanup: again, ONLY targeted namespaces
            if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
              const $w = jQuery(window), $d = jQuery(document);
              [
                'scroll.wpDataTables','resize.wpDataTables',
                'scroll.datatables','resize.datatables',
                'scroll.fixedHeader','resize.fixedHeader',
                'scroll.responsive','resize.responsive',
                'scroll.dtfh','resize.dtfh'
              ].forEach(ns => { $w.off(ns); $d.off(ns); });
            }

            // Harden wpDataTables settings (no auto width reflows)
            if (window.wpDataTables) {
              Object.keys(window.wpDataTables).forEach(function(tableId) {
                try {
                  const settings = window.wpDataTables[tableId].fnSettings && window.wpDataTables[tableId].fnSettings();
                  if (settings) {
                    settings.bAutoWidth = false;
                    settings.responsive = false;
                  }
                } catch(e) {}
              });
            }

            console.log('GCBC: SAFE throttling complete');
          }, 2000);
        }
      });
    })();
    </script>

    <script>
      (function () {
        function killSkeletons() {
          var charts = document.querySelectorAll('[id^="wpDataChart_"], .wpDataChart');
          charts.forEach(function (el) {
            // If the chart has rendered (we see a canvas/SVG), remove obvious placeholders nearby
            var hasRendered = !!el.querySelector('svg, canvas, .apexcharts-canvas, .highcharts-container');
            if (!hasRendered) return;
            // siblings immediately before/after with common placeholder class names
            var sibs = [el.previousElementSibling, el.nextElementSibling];
            sibs.forEach(function (s) {
              if (!s) return;
              var cls = (s.className || '').toString().toLowerCase();
              if (/skeleton|placeholder|shimmer/.test(cls)) {
                s.style.display = 'none';
                s.style.visibility = 'hidden';
                s.style.opacity = '0';
              }
            });
          });
        }

        function disableChartAnimations() {
          // Highcharts
          if (window.Highcharts && Highcharts.setOptions) {
            try {
              Highcharts.setOptions({
                chart: { animation: false },
                plotOptions: { series: { animation: false } }
              });
            } catch (e) {}
          }
          // ApexCharts
          if (window.Apex && window.Apex.chart) {
            try {
              window.Apex.chart.animations = { enabled: false };
            } catch (e) {}
          }
        }

        if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
          disableChartAnimations();
          killSkeletons();
        } else {
          window.addEventListener('load', function () {
            disableChartAnimations();
            // Run twice in case builders inject late
            killSkeletons();
            setTimeout(killSkeletons, 400);
          });
        }

        // Also clean up whenever a chart container mutates (re-render)
        var mo = new MutationObserver(function (muts) {
          for (var i = 0; i < muts.length; i++) {
            var el = muts[i].target.closest && muts[i].target.closest('[id^="wpDataChart_"], .wpDataChart');
            if (el) killSkeletons();
          }
        });
        document.querySelectorAll('[id^="wpDataChart_"], .wpDataChart').forEach(function (el) {
          mo.observe(el, { childList: true, subtree: true });
        });
      })();
    </script>

  /* Minimal safety: make sure chart boxes aren't zero-height and stay visible */
  [id^="wpDataChart_"], .wpDataChart, [class*="wdt-chart"] {

<script id="gcbc-charts-lite">
if (!window.__gcbcChartsLite) { window.__gcbcChartsLite = true; (function(){
  const SEL = '[id^="wpDataChart_"], .wpDataChart, [class*="wdt-chart"]';
  const isHidden = () => document.hidden === true;

  let containers = [];
  function refreshContainers(){ containers = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(SEL)); }
  let ro = null, roAttached = false;
  function attachRO(){
    if (!('ResizeObserver' in window)) return;
    if (!ro) ro = new ResizeObserver(() => { if (!scrolling) syncHeights(); });
    if (roAttached) return;
    containers.forEach(el => {
      const target =
        el.querySelector('.highcharts-root svg') ||
        el.querySelector('.highcharts-container') ||
        el.querySelector('.apexcharts-canvas') ||
        el;
      if (target) { try { ro.observe(target); } catch(_){} }
    });
    roAttached = true;
  }
  function detachRO(){ if (ro && roAttached){ try { ro.disconnect(); } catch(_){} roAttached = false; } }

  // Coalesce layout work to avoid scroll-jank
  let scrolling = false;
  let scrollIdleTimer = null;
  let rafSync = null;

  function scheduleSync(delay = 60){
    if (rafSync) return;
    rafSync = requestAnimationFrame(()=>{
      rafSync = null;
      if (!scrolling){
        setTimeout(syncHeights, delay);
      }
    });
  }

  function scheduleNudge(delay = 100){
    clearTimeout(scheduleNudge._t);
    scheduleNudge._t = setTimeout(()=>{
      if (!scrolling){ nudge(); }
    }, delay);
  }

  function killShimmer(node){
    try { let p=node; while(p){ if(p.classList && p.classList.contains('progresson')){ p.classList.remove('progresson'); p.style.background='transparent'; } p=p.parentElement; } } catch(_){ }
  }

  function prepBox(el){
    if (!el) return;
    if (el.__gcbcPrepped) {
      // Still ensure min-height tracks upwards, but don't touch other styles repeatedly
    } else {
      el.__gcbcPrepped = true;
      killShimmer(el);
      el.style.display   = 'block';
      el.style.visibility= 'visible';
      if (el.parentElement){
        el.parentElement.style.visibility= 'visible';
      }
    }
    const h = Math.max(420, el.clientHeight || el.getBoundingClientRect().height || 0);
    el.style.minHeight = h + 'px';
    el.style.height    = '';          /* DO NOT lock height — allow growth */
    // Removed parentElement minHeight setting as per instructions
  }

  function measureInnerHeight(el){
    // Prefer rendered chart containers
    const n =
      el.querySelector('.highcharts-root svg') ||
      el.querySelector('.highcharts-container') ||
      el.querySelector('.apexcharts-canvas') ||
      el.querySelector('svg') ||
      el.querySelector('canvas');
    if (n) {
      // offsetHeight avoids a forced style+layout read in most cases
      const h = n.offsetHeight || n.getBoundingClientRect().height || 0;
      return Math.ceil(h);
    }
    const h2 = el.offsetHeight || el.getBoundingClientRect().height || 0;
    return Math.max(420, Math.ceil(h2));
  }

  let _syncLock = false, _lastSync = 0;
  function syncHeights(){
    if (scrolling || isHidden() || _syncLock) return;
    const now = Date.now();
    if (now - _lastSync < 80) return;
    _lastSync = now;
    _syncLock = true;
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      containers.forEach(el => {
        const innerH = Math.max(420, measureInnerHeight(el));
        const target = innerH + 12; // small buffer
        if (!el.__gcbcMinH || Math.abs(el.__gcbcMinH - target) > 3){
          el.style.minHeight = target + 'px';
          el.style.height = ''; // keep flexible
          el.__gcbcMinH = target;
        }
      });
      _syncLock = false;
    });
  }

  function nudge(){
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      try {
        // Highcharts reflow if present
        if (window.Highcharts && Array.isArray(window.Highcharts.charts)) {
          window.Highcharts.charts.forEach(c => { try { c && c.reflow && c.reflow(); } catch(_){} });
        }
      } catch(_){}
      // After library reflow, sync with actual rendered content
      setTimeout(syncHeights, 48);
      setTimeout(syncHeights, 240);
    });
  }

  function onReady(fn){ document.readyState!=='loading' ? fn() : document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', fn); }

  onReady(()=>{
    refreshContainers();
    // Initial prep + sync
    containers.forEach(prepBox);
    syncHeights();
    attachRO();
    scheduleNudge(80);

    // Nudge again shortly after for late library paints
    scheduleNudge(800);
    attachRO();

    // Removed original ResizeObserver block as per instructions

    // IntersectionObserver updated as per instructions
    if ('IntersectionObserver' in window){
      const io = new IntersectionObserver((ents)=>{
        if (scrolling) return;
        const newlyVisible = ents.filter(e=>e.isIntersecting).map(e=>e.target);
        if (newlyVisible.length){
          newlyVisible.forEach(prepBox);
          scheduleSync(80);
        }
      }, {threshold: 0.05});
      containers.forEach(el=>io.observe(el));
    }

    // Watch for builders/ads adding chart containers later
    const mo = new MutationObserver(muts=>{
      const need = muts.some(m=>Array.from(m.addedNodes||[]).some(n=> n.nodeType===1 && (n.matches?.(SEL) || n.querySelector?.(SEL))));
      if (need){
        refreshContainers();
        containers.forEach(prepBox);
        scheduleSync(120);
      }
    });
    mo.observe(document.body, {childList:true, subtree:true});

    // Final sweep after late layout shifts
    window.addEventListener('load', ()=>{
      setTimeout(()=>{ containers.forEach(prepBox); scheduleSync(60); }, 600);
    });

    // Keep in sync during window resizes
    window.addEventListener('resize', () => { scheduleSync(80); });

    // Pause aggressive layout work while scrolling; resume shortly after
    window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
      if (isHidden()) return;
      scrolling = true;
      detachRO();
      clearTimeout(scrollIdleTimer);
      scrollIdleTimer = setTimeout(()=>{
        scrolling = false;
        refreshContainers();
        attachRO();
        scheduleSync(60);
      }, 220);
    }, { passive: true });
  });
})(); }

            $(window).off('scroll.wpDataTables');

    <script>
    // Guard: avoid height writes while actively scrolling
    window.__gcbcScrolling = false;
    (function(){
      var __idleTimer;
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function(){
        window.__gcbcScrolling = true;
        clearTimeout(__idleTimer);
        __idleTimer = setTimeout(function(){ window.__gcbcScrolling = false; }, 200);
      }, { passive: true });
    })();
    (function () {
      function setContainerHeight(el) {
        if (!el) return;
        // Prefer the rendered SVG height; fallback to canvas box
        var svg = el.querySelector('svg');
        var h   = 0;
        if (svg) {
          var r = svg.getBoundingClientRect();
          h = Math.ceil(r.height);
        } else {
          var box = el.getBoundingClientRect();
          h = Math.ceil(box.height);
        }
        if (h > 0) {
          var pad = 24; // small breathing room
          var target = h + pad;
          // Only ever raise the min-height during interaction; never shrink mid-scroll
          var prev = parseInt(el.getAttribute('data-minh') || '0', 10);
          if (!window.__gcbcScrolling) {
            var next = Math.max(prev, target);
            if (next !== prev) {
              el.style.minHeight = next + 'px';
              el.setAttribute('data-minh', String(next));
            }
          }
          // Do NOT set a fixed height; keep layout flexible
          el.style.height = '';
        }
      }

      function fixAll() {
        document.querySelectorAll('[id^="wpDataChart_"]').forEach(setContainerHeight);
      }

      // Run after load & on resize
      if (document.readyState === 'complete') fixAll();
      else window.addEventListener('load', fixAll);

      window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
        clearTimeout(window.__gcbcResizeTimer);
        window.__gcbcResizeTimer = setTimeout(function(){
          if (!window.__gcbcScrolling) fixAll();
        }, 180);
      }, { passive: true });

      // Watch for re-renders from the chart libs
      var mo = new MutationObserver(function(muts){
        for (var i=0;i<muts.length;i++) {
          var n = muts[i].target;
          if (n && n.nodeType === 1) {
            var el = n.closest && n.closest('[id^="wpDataChart_"]');
            if (el) setContainerHeight(el);
          }
        }
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('[id^="wpDataChart_"]').forEach(function(el){
        mo.observe(el, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      });
    })();
    </script>
